We need our community to come together more now than ever during this 
cov-19 crisis.   If you are able to please connect with your neighbors 
who maybe self isolating and see if they need assistance.   And likewise 
if you are self isolating and need assistance please reach out and ask 
for help. There's a lot of community support groups out there already 
but if you're not sure drop us a message and we will point you in the 
right direction to help or get help.


Good Neighbours Network

[https://www.goodneighbours.org.uk/good-neighbours-network 
<https://www.goodneighbours.org.uk/good-neighbours-network?fbclid=IwAR18BqHnEz8iEmL9ZXGE-sVpCRpawtlkRVNnDbtaFBsdQWF3BqsRWzuRaNA>](https://www.goodneighbours.org.uk/good-neighbours-network… 
<https://www.goodneighbours.org.uk/good-neighbours-network?fbclid=IwAR0J-6hGngXBE_Xs-6wjTFkWWWEaYTJv8k06kgU-hjfg8mwKwymS9DPwxAo>)


WAM Get Involved

[http://rbwm.communitydatabase.co.uk 
<http://rbwm.communitydatabase.co.uk/?fbclid=IwAR24ruc8kxrKW7k1-imQ7zSOeW1i0ad3T-yb2Id2d8aZjGGy6bEbMs7Lc3o>](http://rbwm.communitydatabase.co.uk/… 
<http://rbwm.communitydatabase.co.uk/?fbclid=IwAR3wMvepbH_OiOoNsboB0q_41K9Pf8FvcVnW25R_XEhAuLRZJwUHb3r4BSI>)


Ward Royal Residents Association
